Jiangsu Provincial Social Education Organizations

Submit Relief Measures for Provincial Education Funds: The directors of provincial social education organizations, due to the heavy floods this year and the shortage of provincial revenue, leading to long-standing arrears in the funding of various organizations and economic hardship that is difficult to support, held a meeting in the province the other day and decided to jointly send letters to the Education Funding Committee, the provincial government, and the Ministry of Education, proposing relief measures for education funds in the province. The relevant official documents are recorded below:

A submission regarding the increasingly tight Jiangsu education funding, respectfully submitting remedial measures for review and implementation. It is found that the main reason for the Jiangsu education funding shortfall is the under-collection of the annual land tax allocation and the impact of the floods on the reliable revenue for the 20th year, which is only about 2 million yuan. After deducting the over 900,000 yuan of arrears from previous years, the net income for the 20th year is only about 1.3 million yuan. This is insufficient to cover the 3.3 million yuan in expenditure. Now that the fiscal year has begun for four months, the education institutions have received less than a month's worth of funding, with arrears of more than three months. If remedial measures are not planned early, there is a risk of schools being suspended soon. The undersigned are currently serving in Jiangsu provincial education institutions and have witnessed the difficulties in education funding. We dare not remain silent and respectfully submit three remedial measures as follows, respectfully requesting your consideration:

1. It is necessary to firmly request the Ministry of Finance to fulfill its commitment to make up the shortfall in land tax revenue for the four years prior to the 19th year. The biggest reason for the shortage of Jiangsu education funding is that the cigarette tax revenue was transferred to the Ministry of Finance in the 16th year of the Republic, and a land tax allocation of 1.8 million yuan was used to offset it. Although it was agreed at the time that the Ministry of Finance would make up for any shortfall, since the 16th year, the annual shortfall has been about 600,000 yuan, and the total shortfall for four years is over 2.5 million yuan. Although repeated requests have been made to the Ministry of Finance for compensation, not a single penny has been allocated. On July 23 of this year, the Ministry of Finance sent a letter to the Executive Yuan Secretariat regarding Jiangsu education funding, stating that the Jiangsu education funding has been approved under the province's land tax item, with a monthly allocation of 150,000 yuan. All shortfalls under the land tax item should be the responsibility of the provincial government to effectively reorganize the land tax to make up for it. Previous letters from your office and the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office have been replied to accordingly, and the Jiangsu Provincial Government has been consulted to urge the Finance Department to earnestly reorganize the province's land tax to prevent any shortfall in special education funds. A detailed analysis of this letter shows that it does not deny the agreement that the Ministry of Finance would make up for any shortfall in the land tax allocation of the 16th year. The advice to the provincial government to urge the Finance Department to earnestly reorganize the land tax to prevent any shortfall in special education funds shows that the Ministry of Finance attaches great importance to special education funds. However, this can only be done for this year and beyond. The 2.5 million yuan of significant funds that have already been collected in the previous four years should still be fulfilled by the Ministry of Finance according to the agreement. There are three reasons for this: Since the land tax allocated from the 16th year has had an annual shortfall of about 600,000 yuan, while the cigarette tax collected by the Ministry of Finance has been increasing year by year and is a large sum, making up for the shortfall is not unfair (Reason 1). Assuming that from the 20th year, the Jiangsu provincial land tax is reorganized by the Finance Department, and the annual special education funds of 1.8 million yuan are fortunately no longer in short supply, the funds already short-collected before the 19th year will still be unavailable. Moreover, the disaster in Jiangsu province this year is extremely severe, and the existing revenue is still uncertain. Therefore, the Ministry of Finance should fulfill its commitment and fully compensate for the 2.5 million yuan in short land tax allocations for the four years before the 19th year to alleviate the current difficulties in Jiangsu education funding (Reason 2). Furthermore, after the promulgation of the Regulations on Trial Implementation of the Budget for the 19th Year of the Republic of China and the Standards for Dividing National and Local Revenue and Expenditure, since the 19th year, land tax has been completely allocated to local revenue. Even if revenue increases due to earnest reorganization, it will not be possible to withdraw any amount to offset the shortfall in land tax allocations under education funding in previous years. This is extremely clear (Reason 3). In summary, education is a fundamental national policy, and the central and local financial authorities should have the responsibility to maintain it. Since Jiangsu education funding has been in a shortfall since the cigarette tax revenue was transferred to the Ministry of Finance in the 10th year of the Republic, with the accumulated arrears reaching a huge 2.5 million yuan, making ends meet is extremely difficult. The Ministry of Finance should, based on the old agreement, the Regulations on Trial Implementation of the Budget for the 19th Year, and the current practical difficulties in Jiangsu, share the difficulties and enthusiastically maintain it, allocating the accumulated arrears in one lump sum or in installments in cash, or using treasury bills to offset the entire amount, so as to alleviate the current difficulties in Jiangsu education funding.

Zhang Yiyan Takes Office as Principal of Nanching

The position of Principal of Jiangyin Nanching Middle School has been vacant for a long time since Zhang Zhongyou left the school. The department insisted that he must act as a short-term acting principal no matter what. There are still over 3,000 yuan in the school's account, which can only last for one month. After arriving at the school, he could not talk about a fundamental solution to the school's policy at the moment. (1) Supplementing the curriculum, (2) financial management, (3) teachers and students must be united in sincerity. The meeting ended.

Outline of the Implementation Principles of Sanmin Zhuyi Education (8) by the Party Department

Chapter 7: Overseas Chinese Education

Section 1: Goals

1. To unify and develop overseas Chinese education based on the purpose of Chinese education and its implementation policy.

2. In light of the special environment of overseas Chinese, in order to improve the international standing of overseas Chinese and promote equality between Chinese and foreign nations, efforts should be made from the educational aspect to enhance the national consciousness of overseas Chinese, train the self-governance ability of overseas Chinese, improve the lives of overseas Chinese, and cultivate productive capacity.

3. Based on the actual situation of overseas Chinese education, efforts should be made to improve and develop overseas Chinese general education, vocational normal education, social education, and supplementary education.

Section 2: Implementation Guidelines

1. Curriculum

I. Same as domestic schools at all levels.

II. Emphasis on knowledge and skills necessary for local life in order to cultivate the ability to survive overseas.

III. In addition, there are seven points that should be given special attention:

(1) the relationship between national migration and nationalism, (2) the relationship between overseas Chinese self-governance and democracy, (3) the relationship between overseas Chinese economic undertakings and people's livelihood, (4) the relationship between overseas Chinese and the national revolution, (5) the relationship between colonial undertakings of various countries and overseas Chinese, (6) the relationship between Japanese southward expansion and the survival of overseas Chinese, (7) the relationship between the world's small and weak nations and Sanmin Zhuyi.

2. Moral Education

I. Same as domestic schools at all levels.

II. Students must understand the local environment and their own position in order to fulfill the mission of developing Chinese overseas.

III. In addition, there are four points that should be given special attention:

(1) to cultivate their national morality with the inherent culture of China, (2) to pay attention to physical exercise in order to adapt to overseas survival, (3) to give more lectures on domestic current events in order to arouse their spirit of loving the motherland, (4) to evoke their attitude towards individuals, families, society, the country, and the international community based on concrete facts related to Sanmin Zhuyi and overseas development.

3. Equipment

I. Same as domestic schools at all levels.

II. To be suitable for the local environment.

III. In addition, there are five points that should be given special attention:

(1) More books, charts, and specimens related to Chinese cultural relics should be prepared, (2) more national product samples should be displayed, (3) more books and charts related to overseas Chinese undertakings should be prepared, (4) more statistical tables and specimens of local products should be displayed, and (5) more books and charts on local history, geography, politics, economy, law, transportation, industry, and commerce should be prepared.

Chapter 8: Concerning Dispatching Students Abroad

Section 1: Objectives

1. Must integrate the strengths of Eastern and Western cultures based on the spirit of the Three Principles of the People, to create a new culture of the Three Principles of the People.

2. Must closely address China's academic needs to cultivate specialized talents in various academic fields.

3. Must closely address China's material needs to cultivate construction talents for various social undertakings.

Section 2: Implementation Outline

1. Publicly funded students abroad must be graduates of universities or specialized schools, without any speeches or actions that violate the Three Principles of the People, and must be dispatched only after passing an examination.

2. Privately funded students abroad must be graduates of high schools or above, without any speeches or actions that violate the Three Principles of the People, and can only go abroad after passing an examination.

3. Regardless of whether they are publicly or privately funded, the academic status and speeches and actions of students studying abroad should be strictly assessed by the relevant competent authorities, and the assessment methods will be determined separately. (End)

A Chinese Initiative to Participate in a Charity Western Boxing Tournament

Guo Huide and Two Others to Dedicate Their Skills on the 5th and 6th of Next Month

At the Wanguo Shangtuan Hall on Fuzhou Road

Western sports, such as football, basketball, volleyball, tennis, and track and field, have been practiced by Chinese people for a considerable period of time. They compete with Europeans and Americans every year, and the results are not weak. However, Western boxing is still unprecedented. Now, three Chinese people, Guo Huide, Zeng Miancai, and Pang Panfang, are scheduled to compete against three Westerners in a charity boxing match at the Wanguo Shangtuan Hall on Fuzhou Road on November 5th and 6th. It is a Shanghai initiative for Chinese to step into the ring. It is expected that there will be a grand occasion at the time.

Guo Huide's Boxing History

Guo Huide learned this skill in the United States. When he was studying in the United States, he served as the captain of the school's boxing team. After returning to China, due to his father's opposition, he has not worn gloves for four years. Recently, seeing the launch of a charity boxing competition in Shanghai, he obtained his father's consent and opened a class in the John's school to practice, inviting Ding Gelianding as a coach (Ding was the former Australian national intermediate champion). Up to 50 people joined, which was quite enthusiastic. This was only two months ago.

Pang Panfang and Zeng Miancai

Pang and Zeng are the best in the class, each weighing 116 pounds. They will compete with two amateur boxers (Westerners). Guo weighs 130 pounds and will fight against a boxer from the British Army. This is the first time that Chinese people have participated in boxing matches. It is hoped that compatriots will come to the venue to watch and cheer.

The Difference Between Chinese and Western Boxing

It should be noted that Western boxing is different from Chinese boxing. In terms of advantages and disadvantages, this technique has been studied by scientific methods. It does not require years of practice. Due to the restrictions of the rules during the competition, both sides can strike hard without the risk of injury. With two or three months of practice, one can learn various fighting skills and can prepare for self-defense at ordinary times, which is a useful sport.

The Competition is Scheduled for the 5th and 6th

The competition is scheduled to be held on November 5th and 6th at the Wanguo Shangtuan Hall. Tickets are priced at 20 yuan, 10 yuan, 5 yuan, 3 yuan, and 1 yuan. All proceeds will be used for flood relief. Ticket sales locations: (1) National Sports Association, (2) Shixiang Trading Company, (3) Huadong Sports Equipment Company.

Free Talk

Anti-Japanese Voice

— Yang Yixiao

Eating Japanese seafood is like drinking poison; eating Japanese white sugar is like taking arsenic. Absolutely untouchable.

Japanese bandits throw bombs. If our 400 million compatriots unite and use our bodies as shields, sacrificing our lives, how can we not defeat the enemy?

Japanese warships are at coastal ports, more every day. If only Zhou Yu were reborn, like Cao Cao's defeat at Red Cliff, he could burn them to the ground, leaving not a single piece of armor.

Violent Japan acts wildly, slaughtering our people. Let everyone vent their anger, turn it into poisonous gas, and poison them to death one by one.

If you don't remove the grass in the courtyard, you will never learn anything.

Faraday

A young friend read "The Death of Edison" and asked me to tell him more about Faraday, Michael Faraday, the inventor of the generator. I am happy to answer this, even more than watching a movie.

Faraday was born in 1791 and died in 1867, living to the age of 76. He invented the principle of the generator at the age of forty (October 17, 1831). With the invention of the principle of the generator, people like Edison were able to use it to create electric lights, streetcars, telephones, and various electrical machines. More people in the world know Edison than Faraday. Before Faraday, electricity could only be considered a scientific trick. Since Faraday invented the generator, the world has changed. Faraday is undoubtedly the founder of the electrified century.

Faraday's father was a blacksmith. He thought that schooling had nothing to do with blacksmithing, so he never sent Faraday to school. At the age of thirteen, Faraday began working as an apprentice to Riebau to learn bookbinding. He learned this job for seven years. He was considered a strange apprentice. He bound books while reading. When the books were bound, he had also finished reading them. Riebau was a knowledgeable master and never stopped his apprentice from reading. During this period, he bound an encyclopedia, which contained an article on electricity. He devoured it at once. He said that this strange electricity did not take much time to read, because there was still much to be known about the principles of electricity. From then on, he had a grand ambition to attack electricity. He also encountered a chemistry experiment book, which he also devoured. He saved money and bought instruments and chemicals to do chemistry tricks. One day, he heard that Davy, a famous chemist at the Royal Society, was going to give a public lecture in London. There was a customer who asked this customer if he could do him a favor and invite him to London to listen to the lecture. This customer readily agreed and bought four admission tickets for him. Faraday went to the city to listen to the lecture, taking notes while listening. After returning to the store, he wrote a long letter to Davy, attaching the notes for him to see, and asked for a meeting. Davy replied and asked him to talk. He boldly asked Davy to give him some work at the Royal Society so that he could learn science. This bold request was generously granted a month later. From then on, Faraday worked as Davy's assistant for a salary of twenty-five shillings a week. This was a major turning point in Faraday's life and a major turning point in the world of learning.

Faraday, generators, the electrified world, all came from a bookbinding apprentice who used both his hands and brain.

Japanese People and Bedbugs

— Feng Wu

The Japanese call bedbugs "Nanjing bugs." The history is like this. Since the beginning of Sino-Japanese trade, Japanese people went to Nanjing to do business. After returning to their country, they found this annoying thing, which later multiplied in Japan. Therefore, the Japanese call it "Nanjing bugs." This shows that Japan does not have this dirty and annoying little animal. Only dirty Chinese people have bedbugs. The implication is to ridicule the Chinese for being unclean and dirty.

When I was studying in Tokyo, I met several Japanese classmates. Among them, one was very representative of Japanese ronin, or the original true face of the Japanese. One day, he took something like a small black bean and showed it to me. With a ferocious smile on his face, he said to me, "Look at this little thing." He giggled and said, "A specialty of China, what do you call it?" I perked up and opened my eyes to see a bedbug. I knew they were here to ridicule the Chinese, so I immediately replied, "This is a Tokyo bug." The three of them looked at each other in a state of panic. Later, I cleverly changed the legend of Nanjing bugs in Japan to the history of "Tokyo bugs." The four of us looked at each other and laughed and dispersed.

How can China alone have mere bedbugs? But the Japanese actually use it to ridicule us Chinese people. It's really hateful.

Wenzhou Karma Records

— Ding Ming

A guest came from Wenzhou and told me two karma stories, both of which have been confirmed in modern times in the area. I believe that they can help save the world and reverse the declining trend, so I record them as follows.

A wealthy man, someone named Jia, was a famous scholar in Wenzhou. He had no children and accumulated millions of wealth, but he regarded money as his life. He was stingy and did not show any pity for the poor. He even levied heavy interest, without any leniency. His neighbor was heavily in debt and had no way to repay it. The wealthy man forced him to sell his pregnant wife to pay off the debt. The neighbors were greatly saddened. On the evening of the wife's departure, she hanged herself. Before she died, she gritted her teeth and said, "After death, I swear to take revenge." When the neighbor committed suicide, it was when the wealthy man's beloved concubine gave birth to a son. Therefore, although the whole family was ecstatic and friends congratulated him, the wealthy man's heart was not happy. When his son grew up, he was arrogant, extravagant, and dissolute, squandering all his property. Before long, the rich family with tens of thousands of acres of fertile land and summer houses was penniless. The wealthy man then regretted and sighed, saying, "People say that if you don't have children, you will be poor in old age. Now I am poor in old age because of my son." He soon died. People thought that he was being punished for breaking up other people's families and couples and for using his superior economic power to oppress the propertyless.

There was also someone named Yi who lived in Wenzhou City and was also a wealthy family. He falsely accused his neighbor's son of a crime, causing the neighbor's son to be wrongly accused. One day, he angrily threw himself into the pond to die. After sleeping, Yi often saw his neighbor's son with disheveled hair, bloody face, and pointing and scolding him with a halberd, saying, "This resentment must be avenged. The revenge is in the shallow pond." The wealthy man Yi was afraid to go to the Qiantang River for the rest of his life. One year, his son went to a university in Hangzhou. During the hot summer, he went into the shallow pond to cool off and drowned. People were surprised, but the wealthy man knew the reason. Later, he told his wife, and the story was passed on, and the whole county knew about it, and they were all frightened by the retribution of karma.

Alas, life is both illusion and reality, both right and wrong. I think there is nothing to say about birth, death, honor, disgrace, wealth, nobility, poverty, or lowliness. Some say that people can conquer nature, but ultimately there is a number. What is there, why should it be said that it is there? What is not there, why should it be said that it is not there? So, those who are ignorant of the true meaning of life and exploit and kill each other, not hesitating to sow evil causes, causing future generations to scold them for hundreds of millions of years, what else is there to say?

— Hai Ke

New Equipment in Train Stations The railway authorities in Cologne, Germany, have added a writing room to the station to make it easier for passengers waiting for trains. It is equipped with typewriters and typists to serve people. For a small fee, you can write letters and send telegrams, which is very convenient. The train station in Frankfurt, Germany, has also added a writing room in the same way because it has seen the popularity of this equipment.

American Consumption The United States is the richest country in the world, so the consumption of Americans is also higher than that of people in other countries. According to recent statistics, they spend an average of 18 pounds and 8 shillings per person in retail food stores and an average of 15 pounds and 12 shillings per person on cars and all car parts. From these two points, it can be seen that Americans love to eat snacks and enjoy sitting in cars.

Prohibition in Chambéry, France The mayor of Chambéry, France, has issued a prohibition that between 10:00 p.m. and 8:00 a.m. every day, no gramophones, pianos, or various sound-producing devices such as radios are allowed in all hotels and public places. People are also notified not to let their dogs bark, and cars in the streets are not allowed to honk their horns, so that everyone in the town can sleep peacefully.

To Fellow Industrial and Commercial Service Workers Amidst National Crisis

— Xin Shui

The Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center, to encourage its successfully placed industrial and commercial service workers, regularly holds service discussion meetings. This meeting coincided with the national crisis. Mr. Pan Yangyao, the head of the center, therefore wrote an article on the contributions of industrial and commercial service workers during the national crisis. The following is a record of the text.

Time flies, and another service discussion meeting is held, only a month after the last one. In this month, violence rages and national disaster looms. Alas, foreign insults increase, and the nation is in turmoil. I know that you all feel pained and resentful to the extreme, and want to rise up to save the country and devise plans to resist violence and ensure survival. There are myriad aspects to saving the country, but in my opinion, there are no more important three points than the following:

(1) Prepare Physical and Academic Strength Our people's physical weakness and lack of spirit are undeniable, and this is especially true for our service industry workers. Usually, there is no opportunity for exercise, and when facing issues, there is a state of timidity. Today, the leaders of the service industry are most dissatisfied with young shop assistants because they are too weak. From now on, we must first pay attention to physical education, exercise our muscles and bones, invigorate our spirits, and sharpen our resolve to prepare our physical strength to jointly face the national crisis. The invaders are deep. If we remain listless today and do not make such preparations, we will only stretch our necks and await the violent slaughter. The foundation of saving the country lies in science. Today, China is not strong enough to compete with violent Japan. Is it because our soldiers are fewer or our food is insufficient? No. When people fight people, victory can be secured. But when science fights science, it is naturally inferior. Not only is visible warfare inferior, but also invisible warfare, such as economic severance. Since boycotting enemy goods, difficulties have been felt everywhere. The lack of raw materials is further ironclad proof of the immaturity of our science. Therefore, today, we must study diligently and delve into science to resist violence and ensure survival. Hu Shi said, "Saving the country should be a penetrating introspection, which can be sustained and strengthened over time." Academic strength is the effort of penetrating introspection.

(2) Strive in One's Respective Position The country is in such a state of decay because everyone is irresponsible, does not strive, and only blames others. We must realize that the country is trampled upon by violent Japan. To our ancestors and descendants, everyone is a great sinner. Therefore, before blaming everything, we should first blame ourselves. Without self-reproach, we cannot save the country. Therefore, our only responsibility today is to strive in our respective positions. More work means more power to resist Japan. More business means more success in saving the country. Producing one more product means resisting enemy goods by one more unit. If we in the industrial and commercial sectors make one more effort in our duties, we will increase our strength in the economic and military battlefields. Mr. Ma Xiangbo, an old man of ninety-two, said, "From now on, the people should each be determined to 'repent of past mistakes, redeem and save ourselves, pool our wisdom and efforts, and jointly face the national crisis. Then, after ten years of recuperation and ten years of education, we will eventually have a day of self-strengthening and revitalization.'" The old man's words should be taken as the standard.

(3) Restrain Desires In the midst of domestic and foreign troubles, natural disasters and man-made calamities, foreign insults have reached this extreme, disgracing our ancestors and harming our descendants. With a mouthful of blood and eyes full of tears, we can only swallow them into our bellies as material for enduring hardship. We have no other way to save ourselves today than to economize on clothing, food, travel, and housing to save China. From now on, we should grit our teeth, make a resolution, stop all kinds of entertainment, and save on all kinds of waste. All unnecessary and non-urgent expenses should be eliminated to prepare for saving the country and resisting violence. Moreover, at a time when the cost of living is rising, we should be keenly aware of the difficulty of maintaining our livelihood, live within our means, and be thrifty and diligent. These eight characters are our golden rule. Gentlemen, the disaster is urgent, the invaders are deep, the country is about to perish, and the race is about to be destroyed. If we continue to be complacent, we may not even have the opportunity to serve in the future. We may not even have the opportunity to gather in a hall like this today. Gentlemen, think about how many people outside the door want to find work but cannot. How many people have no home to return to? How many people have lost their jobs after withdrawing from Japanese businesses? How many people have been unemployed for a long time and are on the verge of desperation? These are all our compatriots. If one person is not able to obtain what he needs, it is our responsibility. What methods do you have to rescue these dying compatriots? Please remember these three words: 1. Prepare physical and academic strength. 2. Strive in one's respective position. 3. Restrain desires.

Letter to the Editor Respectfully, I am writing to you. I recently read in your newspaper's "Voice of Resistance Against Japan" column on the 29th of this month that the main culprits of the alleged collusion between this station and Japan, namely Wei Renming, the director of the reporting department of this station, and two others, have already been dismissed and are under investigation. It is true that Wei Daming, the director of the reporting department of this station, has been suspended from his duties due to certain reasons. However, the alleged collusion with Japan is completely unfounded. Since the Shenyang Incident, this station has recognized the heavy responsibility it bears for international communications and has instructed its subordinates to redouble their efforts to work for the benefit of diplomatic opportunities. The nation is facing a crisis, and everyone with a sense of righteousness is trying to save the country. How could there be such a perverse and reckless act of colluding with the enemy? I am writing to request that your newspaper take immediate steps to correct this information to avoid confusion and to express my sincere gratitude. Respectfully, the International Radio Station of the Ministry of Communications. October 29th.

Yesterday's "Talking About" column by Tingcao Zhai Fu in the "Industrial Civilization" section, on page 12, the character "如" (ru, as) in "如此人間" (ru ci ren jian, such a world) was mistakenly written as "加" (jia, add). This is hereby corrected.

Rotary Club Speaking Tour

A Country Bumpkin Goes to Shanghai Again (Part 2)

— Bao Tianxiao

The country bumpkin set off that day. He actually had experience taking the train. He knew that the ones that were tightly closed on all sides were freight cars, the ones with half of the iron windows open were cattle cars, and that any human being should at least ride in a fourth-class car. He heard people say: taking the train divides people into different classes. Those who ride in first-class cars are first-class people, those who ride in second-class cars are second-class people, and those who ride in third and fourth-class cars are naturally third and fourth-class people. The country bumpkin should ride in a fourth-class car, but the last time he rode in a fourth-class car, he was angered by the vendor of spiced tea eggs. This time, he would be extravagant and ride in a third-class car to show off.

The last time he came back from Shanghai, he was hungry on the train. Just as the spiced tea egg vendor squeezed past him, the aroma of the star anise in the spiced tea eggs tempted him.

"How much does one spiced tea egg cost?" he asked, pretending to be a seasoned gourmet.

"Four for two dimes."

"How can eggs be so expensive? In our village, eggs are only eight copper coins each. Two dimes can buy six." The country bumpkin argued based on his local prices.

"Then smell the aroma. I won't charge you even one copper coin." The spiced tea egg vendor said venomously. Although the country bumpkin's stomach was rumbling, he dared not ask him any more questions. However, the aroma of the spiced tea eggs was deliberately teasing him.

He hated it. He thought that because he was riding in a fourth-class car, even the tea egg vendor looked down on him. Therefore, this time, he was determined to ride in a third-class car.

He strutted to the ticket window, but a person stood there and pushed him, shouting:

"Buy your ticket over there."

He looked up and saw a person wearing a yellow hat, yellow clothes and pants, yellow leather shoes, and a yellow face.

The country bumpkin thought to himself: When I was little, I heard my mother say that the emperor dressed like that, yellow from head to toe, so he was called the emperor. Isn't there no emperor anymore? But his manner and his majesty still seem like an emperor.

"I'm here to buy a ticket," the country bumpkin said boldly.

"Can't you see clearly? This is where first- and second-class tickets are sold." The person in yellow clothes glared at the country bumpkin.

Financial News: Gold Price Drops 9.7 Taels

Treacherous Waters Yesterday, the 20th, the benchmark gold price repeatedly declined, with turbulent waves. At noon, it hovered around 705 taels. In the afternoon, it suddenly broke through the 700-tael mark. The total turnover for the day was 16 taels, which was also substantial. As a result, it plunged by 10 taels. Due to a slight rise in the opening price, the exchange rate rebounded slightly. Subsequently, it stabilized slightly, but as the exchange rate trended towards relaxation, it turned weak again. However, there were occasional underlying currents. The market felt that the exchange rate was particularly loose, and various parties in the market were eager to sell. As the atmosphere deteriorated and the Indian exchange rate rose, the market fell into a weak state. In the face of a sudden storm, the price plummeted by more than 10 taels, from 702.4 taels to within 692 taels. The market was extremely fearful. Later, the Dalian gang and Tongtaichang and others covered their short positions, causing the price to rebound by three or four taels.

The market fluctuated intermittently. It opened in the morning with a drop of 1 tael and 3 mace, at 704.5 taels, with a large bar at another 1/16. The silver price did not move. Subsequently, due to purchases by Hongkangyong, Qianchangxiang, and Tongtaichang, it rose to 07.8 taels. The exchange rate was still loose. HSBC, Yongyu Da, and others sold. The total value of delivered bonds was 46,030,000

Today, the delivery of distant-month futures has been discontinued and physical delivery has been abolished.

The Shanghai Chinese Securities Exchange has suspended trading for three days in order to handle the delivery of bonds and futures. This is because the number of deliveries for October futures contracts for various bonds is still quite large, and the accounting is not as simple as before due to the various related factors such as physical delivery and delivery margin. The total number of deliveries was 46,030,000, of which consolidated tax accounted for the largest share, and the volume of 20-year customs duties, salt tax, and others was also large. The clearing of accounts was handled on Wednesday, and the amount cleared was 6,610,000 yuan. The amount actually delivered was still 39,420,000. There was also a considerable amount of bank custody receipts. Trading will resume at the Securities Exchange today, and new trading in December futures will begin. The restriction on providing physical products for futures selling has been abolished. It is expected that futures contracts for important bonds will be opened. Stabilized Grain Prices in the River Rice Market

Shanghai South: Yesterday, supplies from various sources to Shanghai South were limited, but inventory in Pootung gradually thinned out, and sales in both urban and rural stores were sluggish. Moreover, it was near the end of October in the Gregorian calendar, so firms on both sides were settling accounts, which dampened market sentiment. The price of new japonica rice temporarily stabilized. There was little old kiln-dried Baige rice available, and demand was active, but the limited quantities fetched high prices close to the corner. Supplies of white and wild paddy rice gradually decreased. Although movement in this city was not smooth, prices rose slightly by one or two candareens. Both new imported Du Jian rice were selling at stable prices, and the market was stable. Bian Yin Yuan wine merchants had not yet started operations, so the situation remained stable.

Xin Zha: Yesterday, the rice market in Xin Zha saw more sellers than buyers. Opening prices fluctuated by close to one candareen. The price of top-grade new japonica rice was similar to yesterday. The price of medium-grade rice rose by one candareen. Kiln-dried white paddy rice remained stable. The route for Lu Bu Jian rice was limited. Imported Jian rice was selling quickly, and the price fell by five cents. Demand for glutinous rice was scarce, and the price slightly decreased. Supplies from the interior, including the 24th and 5th varieties and various river factory goods, totaled 4,230 piculs.

Continued New Transactions in Foreign Rice

Yesterday, the foreign rice market saw falling prices and sentiment due to repeated selling by foreign firms. Foreign rice continued to arrive, while demand in this area was limited. Zhen Xing only sold 500 bags yesterday at a price of $10.30. There were few return transactions in forward rice. The opening price for 100 tons of November delivery was 5.1 taels, and the price for 100 tons of April delivery was 5.3 taels. New transactions included Jardine Matheson selling 2,000 tons at only 5.22 taels, for delivery in March and April.

Market for Wheat Flour Strengthens and Then Weakens

Yesterday, the wheat flour market opened with mixed reports of the prices of foreign wheat. Chicago wheat was down about one candareen, while Canadian wheat was up three or four candareens. As a result, initial market sentiment was flat. The market was not actually short of supplies this month, and the initial frenzy had softened. However, deferred delivery months saw active buying due to hurried short covering and general temporary bullishness, causing prices to rise. The market rose by 1.5 cents. In the afternoon, the market opened steadily, but then factories gradually offered to sell, causing external sentiment to gradually weaken. The market fell back by one cent from its highest point. Looking at the market for future months, if flour sales improve, the market should remain stable. As a result, the current month fell by two cents, October fell by 0.75 candareens, December and January each fell by 0.5 candareens, and February and March each fell by 0.25 candareens.

Good Conclusion to the Wheat Futures Market

Yesterday's wheat futures market showed an initial sign of weakness, followed by a strengthening trend. In the morning, foreign wheat prices were mixed, and due to the previous day's excessive gains, both inside and outside traders were hesitant. However, since spot goods had already been withdrawn, the majority of people remained firm, and the market gradually rebounded. By the afternoon, the momentum was even better. The price for November delivery reached a high of 3.8 taels, rising another cent compared to the previous listing. However, the increase was too sharp, and bulls continued to sell. Deferred delivery months were generally stable. As a result, November delivery was up 3 cents from the previous day, December was up 5 cents, January and February were each up 4 cents, and March was up 1 cent.

The current and futures prices of Javanese sugar also remained stable. Both the association market and the designated market saw active buying, and prices rose steadily. The transaction price of Dutch 24th grade raw and white sugar ranged from 11.22 to 11.25 taels; medium white sugar was 10.08 taels; Dutch cotton white sugar ranged from 11 to 11.05 taels. Market sentiment was strong, and Taikoo sugar B mark was traded at 11.22 to 11.25 taels, DY mark at 11.1 taels, HX mark at 12 to 12.05 taels, and HM mark at 11.55 taels. Trading was brisk, and the market was generally strong with potential for further gains. There was active trading in spot raw and white sugar, all for delivery before November, totaling over 4,000 tons. Jardine Matheson sold 500 tons, Yuan Ji sold 1,000 tons, and Hua Xin sold over 1,000 tons, priced at [Dutch currency] 5.575 yuan. Shun Quan Long offered 750 tons, and Jardine Skinner and Bing Chang also offered 300 to 500 tons each, priced at Dutch currency 5.55 yuan, all new regulations plus tax. The firms were taking action due to the expectation that starting in December, there would be a 10% additional tariff, so there were many buyers.

Gradual Price Increase in Black Melon Seeds for Northern and Southern Goods

The price of black melon seeds has been gradually increasing due to tight land prices and scarce arrivals. Market inventory is also low, so prices for both top and bottom grade goods in Shanghai have risen. Recently, Zhongmou seeds were offered at over 17 taels, and the price of Tianjin seeds has risen by two or three taels due to purchases by various firms. Yesterday, the market price for top-grade goods such as Jikui seeds was 24 taels, medium-grade Jizi was 22 taels, and Xukui seeds were 20 taels, ranging down to 19 to 12 taels. Firms with low inventory were watching the market and not selling, with little hope of easing until a large batch of goods arrives.

Zhejiang and Hubei White Filature Silk: 50 Bales Shipped to Shanghai

Preparing to Deliver Period Silk to European Firms at the End of This Month

Zhejiang and Hubei Model Silk Factory's improved white filature silk, with its even color and clean strands, is favored by European and American firms. The amount of silk offered this month is limited. In addition to the silk already delivered, another 50 bales of Datong Bridge and other brands of white filature silk arrived yesterday, preparing for today's delivery of this month's term silk to foreign firms. The factory has already picked up the silk from the Shanghai office for sorting and preparation for today's delivery.

Continued Quiet Sales of European and American Silk

Yesterday, the Shanghai foreign firms' silk market continued to be quiet. Although there were a few Shanghai-bound telegrams for Lyon white filature silk, the offered price actually fell. There was no reply telegram from New York, and the market atmosphere was calm. Yesterday, only [unclear character] Fu and others imported 15 bales of Sichuan yellow filature silk, Samsung imported 3 bales of cotton-spun reeling silk, and Ke Chang and others imported 13 bales of yellow Zusi silk. Prices remained weak.

European Sales of Zhenmei Green Tea are Strong

Yesterday, the foreign firms' tea market in Shanghai saw firms such as Lu Zhuang Tu Zhuang, Jin Long, Yihe, Xiehe, and Yuansheng purchasing Zhenmei green tea, and trading was quite active. Sales of Wu Yuan tea to the US have been sluggish for a long time. Recently, firms such as Hua Cha Jin Jiang have also been purchasing small quantities, but prices have fallen by six or seven to over ten taels. Inventory of Gong Xi tea is also low. Only Zhenmei green tea still has over 10,000 cases in stock, but the route for sales remains sluggish.

Arrival of New Stock of French Wire Nails

Since Sichuan merchants frantically purchased French wire nails, inventory has been depleted. Therefore, those who wanted to replenish their stocks later could hardly find any goods to buy. Yesterday, a new stock of over 4,000 barrels arrived at Pootung's New Taikoo Warehouse, revitalizing the market. The asking price for all types is estimated at 8.75 taels, while the price for a single bundle is 2 or 3 mace higher.

Prolonged Slump in Pig Lead

Since the export merchants stopped purchasing pig lead, the market has been quiet for a long time. Although various colleagues have been trying hard to sell, the sales route is not smooth. Furthermore, domestic lead is frequently arriving, and overseas prices have weakened, making the market particularly weak. The estimated price is 14.75 taels per sheet, and the price of domestic lead is estimated at 14.5 taels.

Sharp Decrease in Datong Coal Arrivals

Since the boycott of Japanese coal, sales of Datong briquette and flake coal in Shanghai have been quite brisk. However, in the past two weeks, arrivals have decreased sharply, leading to a severe shortage of coal in various warehouses. The reason for this is that the water level in Tianjin is currently low, making loading difficult. As a result, the market price for sales has also been unusually firm. Yesterday, the market price was 16.75 taels per ton for screened briquette coal, 16.25 taels for standard coal, and 13.75 taels for coal flakes.

Hong Kong Telegram: Arrival of sea cucumber is very scarce, and prices in various shops have risen by ten dollars.

Ningbo News: Due to mountain merchants selling small amounts, the market price for dried baby octopus has risen to 44 yuan.

Local News

Yesterday's Fourth Preparatory Meeting of Beijing-Guangdong Representatives

Principles of Central Political System Reform Plan Passed

Discussion Continues Today

Representatives of Both Sides Telegraph Central Party Headquarters

Fourth National Congress Postponed

Representatives from Beijing and Guangdong held their fourth preparatory meeting yesterday morning at 9:00 AM in the same location. Li Shizeng and Zou Lu were absent due to illness. The principles of the central political system reform plan have been completely passed. Detailed methods will be further discussed in today's fifth preparatory meeting. A summary of yesterday's proceedings is recorded below:　　Minutes of the Fourth Meeting　The general assembly released the minutes of the fourth meeting yesterday as follows: Representatives present: Wu Chaochu, Zhang Jingjiang, Cai Yuanpei, Li Wenfan, Wang Zhaoming, Sun Ke, Chen Youren, Zhang Ji, Chen Mingshu; Chairman: Wu Chaochu; Recording Secretaries: Zhong Tianxin, Qiu Jinxian, Yang Zongjiong, Cheng Zhonghang. Proceedings were conducted as usual. Resolutions: (1) All news released by this meeting must be agreed upon by all representatives, signed by the chairman of the day's meeting, and handed over to the journalists for publication. The external reports of the meeting's discussion process differ greatly from the facts, which inevitably leads to misunderstandings. A statement should be made. (2) Representatives from both sides should telegraph their respective central party headquarters to request a temporary postponement of the Fourth National Congress, and the date should be set after both sides have reached an agreement. (3) The principles of central political system reform have been passed (Principles): (A) To enable the five Yuans to be independent and responsible and to exercise their powers to realize the spirit of the five-power constitution; (B) To simplify the political system and organization to increase political efficiency and avoid the problems of duplication, circuitousness, and dispersed responsibility; (C) To make political democratization practical, the central political organs should add elected members to make the relationship between the government and the people increasingly intimate and to jointly bear the goal of establishing constitutional government. (4) It was decided to hold the fifth meeting at 9:00 AM on October 31 to continue the discussion of the central political reform plan.

Situation During the Meeting　Of the eleven representatives from Beijing and Guangdong, all attended except Li Shizeng and Zou Lu, who were still absent due to illness. The meeting officially began at approximately 10:00 AM. Before the meeting, the representatives saw the remarks made by a certain Central Committee member from Nanjing in the newspapers, which they believed differed from the facts and could cause misunderstandings. For the sake of a peaceful future, the representatives from both sides carefully studied the matter and drafted a joint statement to be released at the adjournment of the meeting (the statement is recorded separately). The discussion then began and lasted until 12:30 PM. As a result, three items regarding the political system reform plan have been passed in principle. It is said that several detailed methods have also been passed and will be released together after the entire meeting approves them today.

Jointly Issued Statement　Zhang Ji and Cai Yuanpei, representatives of the Central Government to Guangdong for peace negotiations, together with Guangdong representatives Wang Jingwei, Sun Ke, Wu Chaochu, Li Wenfan, and others, issued a joint statement saying: "Recently, we saw in the newspapers that a certain Central Committee member from Nanjing said that the telegram to retire from office was based on the original proposal from Hong Kong at the time, and that it was originally agreed to abolish the Guangdong government after the agreement was reached. It was originally set before the agreement was reached, and then changed to after the agreement was reached in Shanghai, etc. After checking the draft telegrams of both parties that were drafted at that time, we saw that there was no mention of 'before the agreement' or 'after the agreement' in the newspapers, and both parties agreed to release them at the same time. The formal release date has not yet arrived, and whether there will be any revisions in the wording when it is released in the future is another question. Based on the facts at the time, we jointly and responsibly declare this to avoid misunderstandings." Wang Jingwei, Sun Ke, Wu Chaochu, Zhang Ji, Cai Yuanpei, Li Wenfan, October 30.

Guangdong Representatives' Telegram　Guangdong representatives Wang Jingwei, Sun Ke, and others jointly issued a telegram yesterday, saying: "To all national organizations, party departments at all levels, and comrades: Since Zhao Ming (Wang Jingwei) and others arrived in Shanghai, we have received telegrams from some organizations and comrades, saying that we should be united against foreign enemies and go to Nanjing as soon as possible. We came here with the utmost sincerity to seek party and government unity and national unity. In recent days of meetings, we have made decisions on the guidelines for diplomatic progress, and we have also formally begun to discuss various difficult issues of the party and the country. Why has the party not been united for several years? It is because the democratic centralization system has not yet been restored. Why has the country not been unified? It is because we have not been able to follow the National Reconstruction Program and implement political tutelage to complete democratic politics. All these problems need to be resolved. Only by strengthening the foundation of the country internally can we resist powerful countries externally. In December of the sixteenth year, the preparatory meeting for the Fourth Central Committee Plenary Session was held in Shanghai. The current situation is the same, so the meeting is also being held in Shanghai. In short, the important task of this meeting is to allow free will to be fully expressed and to fundamentally resolve the various difficult issues of the party and the country. We hereby send a special telegram in reply, hoping that you will understand." Wang, Sun, Wu, Li, Zou, Chen, 30th.

Fourth National Congress Postponed　The Guangdong representatives sent a telegram yesterday regarding the postponement of the Fourth National Congress, saying: "To the Extraordinary Meeting of the Central Executive and Supervisory Committees in Guangzhou: It was resolved at today's meeting that representatives from both sides should telegraph their respective central party headquarters to set the date for the Fourth National Congress after both sides have reached an agreement. We hereby report." Wang Zhaoming, Sun Ke, Wu Chaochu, Li Wenfan, Zou Lu, Chen Youren, 30th.

Conversation Meeting at Mr. Hu's Residence　Yesterday afternoon at 4:30 PM, Guangdong representatives Sun Ke, Wang Jingwei, Chen Youren, and others drove to Mr. Hu's residence on Ma'erxi'ai Road to hold a conversation meeting. It had been arranged in advance that Mr. Wu Chaochu would arrive before Mr. Sun and the others. Li Wenfan was also present. After everyone gathered, they had a secret conversation with Mr. Hu Zhantang. It is said that they discussed matters related to the peace conference to promote its early success. They talked for a long time. Mr. Wu left at approximately 6:00 PM, and Wang, Sun, Chen, and others left at approximately 6:30 PM.

Hu Hanmin's Conversation　Yesterday's newspapers reported that a certain Central Committee member in Nanjing advocated that all state affairs should be resolved by the Fourth National Congress and that the Central Committee could designate representatives from the first and second sessions to hold the Fourth National Congress to discuss and decide on state affairs. Reporters specially visited Mr. Hu Zhantang, who has been most active in promoting peace, to inquire about his opinions on this matter. Mr. Hu gave the following remarks: "Seeing that the party and the country are disintegrating and diplomacy is losing its power and humiliating the country, I came to Shanghai with great grief and indignation at the request of both Guangdong and Ningxia to conduct peace talks, hoping to use the unified strength of the whole country as a backing for diplomacy with Japan. After arriving in Shanghai, I immediately sent a telegram urging Guangdong to elect representatives to come north to hold a meeting. After receiving the telegram, Guangdong immediately appointed Mr. Wang, Sun, Wu, and Li as representatives and arrived in Shanghai on October 21. I also agreed in person to hold a meeting in Shanghai and promised to send representatives to Shanghai immediately after the telegram was sent. Later, Mr. Jiang returned to Nanjing first, and the Guangdong representatives sent a letter on that day's meeting results. Mr. Jiang also replied on the 24th, entrusting Mr. Li Shizeng, Zhang Jingjiang, Zhang Puquan, Cai Jiemin, and Chen Zhenru as representatives to meet with the Guangdong representatives. This is the process of opening the peace conference, which should be known to the people of the country. I hope that everyone can be sincere, discuss everything, and decide on two draft telegrams based on the results of the discussion in Hong Kong between Mr. Cai, Zhang, Chen, and Mr. Jingwei and Zhesheng and Mr. Pei San. One is Mr. Jiang's telegram, and the other is the Guangdong government's telegram, advocating that the peace and unity conference should resolve to reorganize the unified government. After the unified government is established, Mr. Jiang will be dismissed, and the Guangdong government will be abolished. The resolution details are based on the plan to organize the unified government to achieve consistency between the north and the south and to seek reform of internal and external affairs and to open up a new path for future politics to comfort the longings of the national masses. However, today, the so-called Central Committee member from the Beijing side suddenly made a statement, advocating that all state affairs should be resolved by the Fourth National Congress and that representatives from the first and second sessions should be designated as representatives to the Fourth National Congress as much as possible. Then, there is almost no need for empty discussions, and we can wait until we are sitting in the National Congress to speak. At the same time, the Nanjing Central News Agency also released news, saying that the negotiation process released in Shanghai differs greatly from the facts and that the original meaning of the past is erased. Chairman Jiang seems to advocate seeking perfection and states that he will listen to the public opinion of the Central Committee and that he will never lightly abandon his responsibility when the country is in trouble. I will not discuss whether the so-called public opinion of the Central Committee and Mr. Jiang's personal advocacy are true. However, based on my speculation, Mr. Jiang should not be untrustworthy because he respects the resolution of this peace conference, which is expected by the whole country, and his personal promises. However, the so-called Central Committee member, I don't know who he is, his destruction of the progress of the peace and unity conference can be said to be meticulous. Since the representatives of Ningxia and Guangdong gathered in Shanghai, the Beijing side first used the name of diplomatic urgency to send a telegram urging me to enter Beijing that night and at the same time issued a declaration supporting the League of Nations to take the Japanese army to withdraw on the 16th of next month. At this time, it is suddenly said that diplomacy is urgent, and urging people to enter Beijing cannot but make people ask questions. Later, the party departments at all levels belonging to the Beijing side sent thousands of identical telegrams urging me to enter Beijing, and when the peace conference discussed and released the telegrams of both parties, some domestic generals planned to send telegrams saying that the head of state should not be easily telegrammed, etc., which made people wonder whether the Beijing side was sincerely negotiating peace. However, the party department is not to blame, because some people may have urged it to do so, so it cannot but obey orders. The military is also not to blame, because in China, where politics and party affairs are controlled by guns and bullets, this kind of article is commonplace. Only the so-called Central Committee member also published this discussion that destroys the peace and unity conference to delay the unity of the country, which cannot but make people horrified. Whether the peace and unity conference will continue to be held in the future, I am not involved in this peace conference, so I am not in a position to speculate. However, my personal opinion is that I hope that both Ningxia and Guangdong can still abide by their promises so that the peace conference can proceed smoothly. At the same time, I hope that they can also make great determination in the reform of diplomacy and internal affairs in the future so that they can achieve success. As for the opinions on convening the Fourth National Congress, I have already expressed them some time ago and will not go into details now."

Zou Lu's Illness Has Slightly Improved　Guangdong representative Zou Lu's illness has slightly improved after being diagnosed and treated by Chinese and Western medicine yesterday. The doctor said that Mr. Zou had a slight fever and a slight pain in his throat, but there was no major problem. He closed his doors to visitors for the past two days. Mr. Zou was unable to attend yesterday morning's fourth preparatory meeting, and he was also unable to attend the conversation meeting at Mr. Hu's residence that night. He will probably recover within a few days.

I am writing this telegram with great sorrow, and I beg you to send condolences to Mr. Gu's family on my behalf." Hu Hanmin kowtows.

Strive to Advocate and Be a Vanguard for the People

Never Buy or Sell Japanese Goods for Life

The Executive Committee of this city issued an order yesterday to the party departments of each district to instruct the subordinate branches to hold an oath-taking ceremony for resisting Japan and saving the country when convening the party member congress. The order and oath are recorded below:

Order: "For the purpose of issuing an order, since the violent Sun invaded and occupied Liaoning and Jilin, the people of the country have hated it with a passion. Committee Meeting to Implement Severance of Relations

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce's committee to implement the severance of economic relations with Japan held its second standing committee meeting yesterday. Chairman Ye Jia and the following resolutions were passed: (1) A letter from the Iron Industry Association stated that Yongji Iron Shop's account books were taken away by the Anti-Japanese Association. They requested intervention for their return. Furthermore, the association's inspectors did not cooperate with the inspection teams and inspected shops of the same trade independently. They requested a letter to correct this. As for whether the inspection teams can collect the Japanese goods sold and stored by businesses in the same trade and report to request disposal, they also requested instructions. Resolved: (1) Send a letter to the Anti-Japanese Association to promptly investigate and

return the account books and records. (2) Send a letter to the Anti-Japanese Association, requiring future inspections of businesses in various industries to be carried out in close cooperation with the inspection teams of each industry. (3) Sealing up Japanese goods is permitted for storage in public warehouses, but the quantity and date of import must be promptly reported. (2) A letter from Xin Kang Coal Shop stated that the Charcoal Industry Association reported that the shop would resume sales with Sanxing, which was not true. They requested verification. Resolved: Forward to the Investigation Section. Encouraging the Acceptance of Chinese Workers from Japanese Factories

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the industry associations yesterday, stating: "Received Instruction No. 327 from the Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee of the Chinese Nationalist Party, which states: 'For your information, the Third District Party Headquarters submitted a report, requesting the establishment of a domestic goods factory to accommodate Chinese workers from Japanese factories. Please adopt and implement this suggestion.' This is of utmost importance.'" Attached was a copy of the submittal to the association. In view of this, and that the severance of economic relations with Japan has been unified nationwide, and that establishing domestic goods factories to accommodate Chinese workers from Japanese factories is a crucial part of the anti-Japanese work, the instruction was recorded along with the original submittal and forwarded to you. It is hoped that your association will take this into account, vigorously promote and widely advise accordingly.

Request to Remove Japanese Merchants' Advertisements from Railways

The Anti-Japanese Association sent a letter to a certain advertising company, stating: "We are writing to inform you that according to reports, countless advertisements for Japanese goods are planted along the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, all of which are handled by a certain advertising company in Shanghai. It has been found that the person in charge of the company also has the obligation and mission to investigate Japanese goods in the same industry. We hereby expose this and request that your association remove them within a limited time and severely punish them as a warning to those who use public office for private gain." As a representative of the same industry, you should first earnestly implement this to set an example for the public. In view of the aforementioned situation, we hereby send a special letter to inform you that all advertisements for Japanese goods along the railways must be removed immediately to show your patriotic enthusiasm and anti-Japanese determination. Please investigate and handle this matter and reply as soon as possible."

In view of this, our association, in addition to compiling a reference list of Japanese medicines and sending it to members, and organizing crash courses in battlefield rescue, has decided at the 12th executive committee meeting of the 5th session on October 25 to print voluntary mobilization forms for enemy defense and self-defense and send them to members to fill out and send back to the association so that they can serve the country in the event of an unfortunate war. This matter concerns the national salvation movement, so please investigate and handle it accordingly." Chinese Merchant Trams Resume This Morning

Treatment Conditions Completely Resolved

Wu Quesheng Agrees to Resign Voluntarily

All Company Employees Return to Work

The Chinese Merchant Electrical Company in this city experienced a strike by all employees, resulting in tram service without ticket sales. After the City Party Department intervened to mediate, a concrete solution was reached. However, it was not approved by the employees' meeting. Yesterday, the Party and government agencies mediated again and decided to follow the instructions. The employees' meeting approved it, considering it satisfactory. They all returned to work at 4:30 PM last night, and tram service has fully resumed this morning. The details are recorded as follows:

Mediation Process: Wu Kaixian, Standing Committee Member of the City Party Department, and Xu Yefu, Head of the Civil Training Section, convened representatives of all employees and representatives of the company the day before yesterday. As a result of the mediation, a solution was reached based on the impartial decision of the Social Affairs Bureau, as follows: Employee salary increase plan (1) Those above 90 yuan will receive an increase of 10%. (2) Those between 50 yuan and 90 yuan will receive an increase of 25%. (3) Those between 36 yuan and 50 yuan will receive an increase of 10%. (4) Those between 12 yuan and 25 yuan will receive an increase of 40%. (5) Those below 21 yuan will receive an increase of 55%. (6) Trainees will be increased proportionally. They also persuaded them to return to work immediately. Later, the employees' meeting discussed that the purpose of the strike, to expel Wu Quesheng, head of the General Affairs Section, had not been achieved, and the meeting adjourned without a result.

Traffic Situation: The First District Water and Electricity Industry Union (i.e., the Chinese Merchant Workers' Organization) and employee representatives held a joint meeting the night before last to discuss measures. Yesterday morning, the union sent all directors and supervisors, Tang Junsheng, Zhou Guangrong, etc., to the company to try to maintain the tram departure. A total of nine trams on Route 1, four trams on Route 2, eight trams on Route 3, and six trams on Route 4. However, because employees continued to strike, ticket sales were suspended. Therefore, the previous day's method of tram service without ticket sales was still followed.

Solution: Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, and Wu Kaixian, Standing Committee Member of the City Party Department, convened representatives of all employees and representatives of the company again at the City Party Department yesterday morning to mediate again. As a result, both parties agreed and decided on the following: (1) Wu Quesheng, Head of the General Affairs Section of the Chinese Merchant Electrical Company, will resign voluntarily. (2) Employee treatment conditions: (A) Those above 90 yuan will receive an increase of 10%. (B) Those between 50 yuan and 90 yuan will receive an increase of 25%. (C) The City Government's instruction to cancel the 30% increase for those between 26 yuan and 50 yuan will be revoked and changed to a 40% increase for those between 21 yuan and 50 yuan. (D) Those below 21 yuan will receive an increase of 55%. (E) Trainees will be increased according to this example, effective from October 20. (3) Ding Ren will be responsible for fulfilling the treatment conditions. At that time, employee representatives stated that the above decisions must be approved by the employees' meeting.

Municipal Government Instructions: The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau received instructions from the Municipal Government yesterday, stating: "Regarding the matter of the Chinese Merchant Electrical Employees' treatment conditions and salary increase plan, the 30% increase for those above 36 yuan is canceled, and they are instructed to resume work as usual." The bureau instructed all employee representatives, Deng Shuping, etc., stating: "To comply with the matter, it was found that the employees jointly requested to improve their treatment. After the bureau decided to instruct them to comply, it was reported that the employees expressed dissatisfaction and suddenly went on strike. We have submitted a report to the Municipal Government for review and adjudication. Now, we have received Instruction No. 12464 from the Municipal Government, reviewing the handling method, etc. Therefore, we are enclosing a copy of the original instruction and sending personnel from the City Party Department to persuade the employees to go to the company to resume work immediately. Please comply strictly." It also instructed the Chinese Merchant Electrical Company, with similar content as above.

Employees' Meeting: At 2 PM yesterday, all employees held an employees' meeting at the Lianyi Society on Guohuo Road. Chairman Shen Yuping, Xu Yefu from the City Party Department, Zhang Shouchun, a clerk from the Public Security Bureau, and Guo Yongxi, a clerk from the Social Affairs Bureau, attended to provide guidance. The chairman first reported on the process, followed by reports from representatives of the Party and government agencies on the mediated solution, and then began discussions after persuading them to return to work. (1) Resolved to approve the treatment conditions. (2) All will return to work immediately. (3) The Maintenance of Order Association will be canceled immediately. (4) Whether the employee representatives should continue to exist was resolved to be retained. (5) Zhu Zhizai's resignation from his position as a representative and from his position at the company was unanimously resolved to be retained.

Full Resumption of Work: All employees of the Chinese Merchant Electrical Company's lighting, transportation, general affairs, clerical affairs, materials, technology, engineering, accounting, and document sections resumed work at the company at 4:30 PM yesterday afternoon after the meeting. However, due to time constraints, tram service on each route did not have time to issue tickets and will remain temporarily without ticket sales. All tram services on each route will resume issuing tickets tomorrow.

Workers' Meeting: All workers of the Chinese Merchant Electrical Company held a representative meeting at the union on Guohuo Road at 9 PM yesterday to discuss measures. All directors and supervisors explained everything and persuaded them to work with peace of mind. It was heard that the company has not yet fulfilled some of the worker treatment conditions that have been signed by both labor and management, such as the 3,000 yuan out of the 5,000 yuan case that the company has not yet issued. Although the company has agreed, it insists that the union send a letter stating.

Addressing the Coal Shortage Problem

Telegraphing the Jiaoji Railway to Retain Price Increases

Telegrams from Commercial Organizations: Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, Shanghai Shipping Association, Chinese Cotton Mill Owners' Association, Shanghai Silk Mill Industry Association, Chinese Seamen's Union Reorganization Committee, Shanghai Copper, Iron, and Machinery Industry Association, Shanghai Oil Mill Industry Association, Shanghai Inland River Steamboat Industry Association, Chinese Marine Engineers' Federation, Chinese Merchant Marine Officers' Association, etc., sent a telegram to the Boshan Mining Industry Association yesterday, stating: "To the Boshan Mining Industry Association, the Jiaoji Railway Bureau plans to increase prices starting tomorrow. Your association has resolved to strike and make a final appeal. Upon hearing this news, our associations are extremely anxious. Shanghai's coal reserves are less than a month. If Lu coal stops, it will open the door for foreign coal to invade and hinder the development of domestic coal, endangering social tranquility and the people's economy. We have now jointly telegraphed the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry, and the Shandong Chairman Han to instruct the Jiaoji Railway to temporarily retain the price increase plan and for the central government to convene representatives from various railways and mine owners to conduct a detailed discussion, so that the freight rates of each railway are equally treated, ensuring that the state benefits, the mine owners bear the burden, and both parties can take care of their own interests. In addition to sending separate telegrams, please do not strike before receiving the government's written order to avoid a coal shortage. This is of utmost importance." (Telegrams to the Beijing-Shandong authorities were reported in yesterday's newspaper.)

Telegram from the National Coal Production and Sales Association: "To the Nanjing National Government Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Railways, we respectfully acknowledge the telegram from the Ministry of Railways yesterday. We have forwarded it to the Shandong Zibo Propaganda Coal Mine Association. We have now received a reply stating: 'The Jiaoji Railway's freight rates are the highest compared to other state-owned railways. For example, the Jinpu Railway charges 5 li per ton-mile to Zhongxing, the Ruoning Railway charges 6 li to Beipiao, and the Pinghan Railway charges 6.825 li to Liuhegou, regardless of exports or domestic. The Jiaolu Railway originally charged 7.3 li for exports, and after the increase, it will be more than 8.1 li. The domestic rate is 1.6 li, averaging more than 1.2 li, which is already more than double that of other railways. The Ministry of Railways' telegram stated that the railway's freight rates are the lowest, which is completely untrue. Coal merchants have repeatedly requested a reduction, but have not been granted it. Previously, in June of this year, we received a telegram from the Ministry of Industry, approving the Ministry of Railways' statement that it had ordered the railway to negotiate fair measures with various coal merchant associations. The coal merchants have repeatedly requested consultations but have not been fulfilled. Now, the price increase is being made unilaterally, which cannot be trusted by the coal merchants. As for the 20% summer rebate, the railway bureau's announcement only stated that the 20% rebate would be implemented, but it was still collected at the original price of 2 yuan and 5 jiao and 2 fen per ton. If calculated according to the 20% rebate method, it should only collect 2 yuan, 4 jiao, and several fen per ton. Now it is still collected at the original price. In fact, the railway bureau has clearly admitted to canceling the price increase, so coal merchants can only comply with the orders of the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Railways and negotiate a fair freight rate with the railway. The Ministry of Railways already knows that the cost of coal mines on the Jiaolu Railway is higher, so state-owned railways should primarily develop industries and should reduce freight rates to show extra preferential treatment. Why do you want to increase prices above the already high freight rates of other railways? Coal merchants are struggling to maintain their business and livelihood. How dare they make things difficult for the railway bureau on purpose? We hereby telegram your government and ministries again, earnestly requesting that you promptly order the Jiaoji Railway Bureau to cancel the price increase to maintain the lack of fuel and benefit the resistance work. Thank you.'" Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the Chinese National Coal Production and Sales Association, and Standing Committee Members Fang Jiaobo, Hong Gubin, Sheng Pihua, and Liu Yumen respectfully bow. (Seal)

The Ministry of Industry Replied Yesterday: "To the Shanghai Chinese National Coal Production and Sales Association, we have received your telegram. In May of this year, the coal merchants of Shandong Zibo and Weifang counties suspended operations due to the Jiaoji Railway's cancellation of the summer rebate. After repeated consultations between our ministry and the Ministry of Railways, we approved the reduction according to the existing summer price reduction method, limited to four months. During this period, both parties should negotiate fair freight rates. Later, due to summer rain disasters and excessive coal costs, we approved the Ministry of Railways' extension of the aforementioned period to the end of October. As the deadline approaches, we are scheduled to transfer the price. On the day of the month, the Shanghai Coal Industry Association telegraphed that the Jiaoji Railway Bureau announced that the coal price

would be increased. The domestic price will be increased by 20%, and the export price will be set at 2 yuan and 8 jiao, effective from November of this year. This move is tantamount to suicide. We telegraphed to order the cancellation of the agreement and to re-negotiate a special price, etc. We have also consulted the Ministry of Railways for verification and handling. We are now reporting to you that the allegations made in the telegram are true. At this time, when we are promoting domestic products, we should eliminate obstacles and vigorously maintain them to promote development. The coal reserves of each ministry are now low and urgently need to be supplemented by domestic coal. Increasing freight rates at this time seems inappropriate. The allegations made in the association's telegram are mostly true. Can you immediately telegraph the Jiaoji Railway Bureau to withdraw the order? Please preside over the handling of this matter. Please be informed."

Map of Japanese Aggression in Northeast China

Now Published

The current "New Japan Cartography," managed by Su Shenrong, has produced various new Chinese and foreign maps over the years, which have been well received by society. Since the Shenyang Incident, it has compiled a "Map of Japanese Aggression in Northeast China." All areas occupied by the Japanese army and areas reached by their airplanes and warships are marked in red. All other county names, cities, towns, and stations are fully displayed. It has now been published and is being sold by Datong Bookstore and Minzhi Bookstore in various cities. Those who wish to purchase more should write directly to the company at No. 19, Baolongfang, Albert Road. It is said that each hundred copies cost 21 yuan.
